        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer204875078" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13975222797230334169"><b>
  <i>Just your average boy-meets-girl, girl-kills-people story.</i>
</b><br/><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Not many authors can scare you to death by eliciting vivid, gruesome imagery and, at the same time, take your breath away with sheer beauty of their prose. I never expected <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4086715.Kendare_Blake' title='Kendare Blake' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kendare Blake</a> to be one of those authors – that’s why her book took me completely by surprise. It was very different from what I thought it would be. When I choose a book based on a beautiful cover and an intriguing title (and yes, I really AM that shallow</span>
  <span id="freeText13975222797230334169" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Just your average boy-meets-girl, girl-kills-people story.</i>
</b><br /><b>4.5 stars</b><br /><br />Not many authors can scare you to death by eliciting vivid, gruesome imagery and, at the same time, take your breath away with sheer beauty of their prose. I never expected <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4086715.Kendare_Blake" title="Kendare Blake" rel="nofollow noopener">Kendare Blake</a> to be one of those authors – that’s why her book took me completely by surprise. It was very different from what I thought it would be. When I choose a book based on a beautiful cover and an intriguing title (and yes, I really AM that shallow), especially one that none of my friends have read, I usually end up disappointed. Anna Dressed in Blood undoubtedly looks amazing and has a memorable title, but the most interesting part is right where it should be – between the covers.<br /><br />Cassius Theseus Lowood grew up in an unconventional family. His mother is a white witch and his father was in the business of killing the dead for the second time, at least until one of the ghosts he was hunting murdered him in the most gruesome way. In Cas’s world, dead people often don’t want to leave the place where they died, especially if they were victims of a violent crime. Instead, they stay behind as monstrous echoes of their former selves – most of them seeking revenge for the horrors they experienced.<br />When Cas’s father died, Cas inherited his duties and his powerful athame. He’s been moving all over the country and killing ghosts since he was 14 years old. But he’s never run into a ghost as powerful as Anna nor did he ever try so hard to understand what drives a dead person to murder innocent people. <br />Anna is different in every way. She was killed in 1958. while walking to the prom in her beautiful white dress. When her throat was slit, blood covered her entirely, thus earning her the name Anna Dressed in Blood. <br /><i>Someone cut her throat, but that’s an understatement. Someone nearly cut her head clean off. They say she was wearing a white party dress, and when they found her, the whole thing was stained red. That’s why they call her Anna Dressed in Blood.</i><br /><br />Ever since her murder, Anna’s been tied to the house she grew up in. Twenty seven people have tried to enter, and none of them came out alive. <br /><br /><br />Nothing is black and white in Anna's story: she is both a killer and a victim, a horrible monster and an innocent girl – and just when you think you figured her out, she turns around and does something completely unexpected! Her entire personality changes as quickly as her appearance which forces Cas to doubt every single choice he made since the beginning of his hunt. <br /><br />I don’t usually watch horror movies and I always do my best to avoid horror novels, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Oh, so what? I live alone and I scare easily. :D <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but black witches, white witches, people trapped in walls, Voodoo, athames, ghost hunting, cursed objects, a strong male protagonist and unexpected developments made me very happy that I decided to read this book. I really hope it gets the attention it deserves.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13975222797230334169" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_210400449" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/210400449" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572638169p2/2016128.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/210400449?book_show_action=true">Sep 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/2016128-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-red">color-red</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=color-black">color-black</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=male-protagonist">male-protagonist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=buy-hard-copy">buy-hard-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=novels">novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2016128-shannon?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer210400449" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10121941542277112064">I'm the first to admit that when something is hyped I give it the ol' stink-eye, and I very rarely enjoy something that's popular or that everyone and their brother tells me I'll like. I pounced on this book before the "ZOMG YOU HAVE TO READ THIS!!1!" crazy train rolled into the station, and I'm really glad I did. <b>This is one of those rare instances where everybody likes a book because it's actually <i>good</i>.</b><br/><br/>I guess I wasn't paying much attention at first glance, mostly to avoid spoilers, but <b>I was </b></span>
  <span id="freeText10121941542277112064" style="display:none">I'm the first to admit that when something is hyped I give it the ol' stink-eye, and I very rarely enjoy something that's popular or that everyone and their brother tells me I'll like. I pounced on this book before the "ZOMG YOU HAVE TO READ THIS!!1!" crazy train rolled into the station, and I'm really glad I did. <b>This is one of those rare instances where everybody likes a book because it's actually <i>good</i>.</b><br /><br />I guess I wasn't paying much attention at first glance, mostly to avoid spoilers, but <b>I was surprised that the protagonist was actually male</b>. I thought Anna was the main character, but even though she's not this is still very much her story. <b>Anna is terrifying.</b> She doesn't fuck around and she doesn't take shit from anyone. She makes you feel sorry for her though, which at first seems like an impossible feat, and yet it definitely happens. <b>It's the sign of a capable author who makes you sympathize with a character who literally tears people apart.</b><br /><br />Cas is the "ghost hunter" and reluctant hero of the story. He's definitely cocksure, but not annoyingly so. He doesn't whine, he doesn't act like an ass, and he doesn't make stupid decisions. <b>Cas is one of the best young male protagonists I think I've ever come across.</b> He's smart and knows his strengths and once he realizes he can't get his job done without the help of others, he accepts it and adapts. <br /><br /><b>The only reason I gave this book 4 stars instead of 5 was because the rhythm of the story stuttered a bit around the halfway point.</b> We're essentially given two climaxes, and after the first one receded I knew it was just a matter of time before the other shoe dropped. There's a scene just before the villain emerges that was probably one of the scariest parts of a book I've ever read, but unfortunately after reading that bit, nothing else could compare. I expected something equally terrifying when Cas finally came face to face with his adversary, but it just didn't happen. Not that the ending and final fight were <i>bad</i>, just that I wanted something <i>more</i>.<br /><br />Blake's writing is beautiful and incredibly lyrical. There were so many quotable passages that I wanted to type out almost a whole page for some of my updates. <b>She writes realistic teenagers without relying on too many stereotypes and clichés, and her characters form believable bonds unlike a lot of stories where a group of kids just randomly band together to save the day.</b> There were casualties along the way, and I liked that I didn't see some of them coming. I also enjoyed the gore and gruesome bits, and I don't think it ever got to the point where someone would be offended or disgusted by some of the graphic violence. It's over quickly, at least, and she does balance the spookier parts with some well-placed humor throughout.<br /><br />I'm excited that she's writing a sequel to this story and I hope she writes other books and other series in the future. Anna and Cas are two of my favorite characters I've read about this year and I can't wait to see what's in store for them. <b>It's so nice to finally read a paranormal young adult book that isn't absolute drivel.</b> Bravo, Blake. Bravo.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10121941542277112064" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_229427738" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/229427738" />
    <a title="Megs ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5691412-megs"><img alt="Megs ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587306329p2/5691412.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/229427738?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Megs ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Megs ♥" href="/user/show/5691412-megs">Megs ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Megs ♥ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/5463965-heidi">Heidi</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5691412-megs?shelf=disappointing">disappointing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5691412-megs?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5691412-megs?shelf=z-2012-reads">z-2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5691412-megs?shelf=cover-lover">cover-lover</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer229427738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17414124955394442770"><br/>Ughh. The first half of this book I would say was a solid 4/5. The second half, unfortunately, put me to sleep. 3/5 stars I guess to balance it out, but right now I feel that is even generous. <br/><br/><br/>When I went into this book I had zero expectations. I think ghosts are cool, and I was really just looking for something super creepy, because that was what I was in the mood for. I didn't even really have anything to compare this to, because I haven't read very many ghost books and have never watched any </span>
  <span id="freeText17414124955394442770" style="display:none"><br />Ughh. The first half of this book I would say was a solid 4/5. The second half, unfortunately, put me to sleep. 3/5 stars I guess to balance it out, but right now I feel that is even generous. <br /><br /><br />When I went into this book I had zero expectations. I think ghosts are cool, and I was really just looking for something super creepy, because that was what I was in the mood for. I didn't even really have anything to compare this to, because I haven't read very many ghost books and have never watched any kind of t.v. shows involving them either. <br /><br /><br />Cas is a ghost hunter and he hates to be called a ghostbuster. lol He wants to avenge his father's death as he was killed by a ghost he was trying to hunt. First, though, he must kill Anna. Anna is a ghost of a girl who was brutally murdered in the 1950s. Anna is epic in my opinion. Cas has some friends to help him with Anna, but as he gets closer to killing her he finds himself starting to like her (wtf?) For me this is when the story just gets ridiculous.<br /><br /><br />Some things I loved in this book were Cas and Anna. Not together. Cas was a pretty cool guy for the most part and I really liked him. Anna was awesome, and at some point I found myself really bored with the story and I was skipping ahead and reading only the parts with Cas and Anna talking. The rest of the school kids weren't that interesting at all.<br /><br /><br />I really enjoyed Anna's back story. It reminded me of being 13 and telling ghost stories when I went camping with my friends, and sure it would have creeped me out for more back then, but it was still a great story. I felt really bad for her, and when everything was revealed about her death I was pretty shocked and pissed off.<br /><br /><br />The bad thing here is that once Anna's story was revealed there were still lots of pages left in this book. Lots of boring pages if you ask me. I didn't really care to read much more about it, and I certainly did not want to read about the romance. It just seemed so silly. This book didn't have any good plot twists or anything intense you would normally expect from a book like this. Even the ending just kind of happened and left no impression on me. I think this book will be forgettable.<br /><br /><br />This is book one of a series, and I can't say I'm excited to start book two as soon as it comes out. I might give it a try, because based on the beginning of the book the story has potential. I'm just afraid the rest is going to be a really bad paranormal romance and that would be disappointing. In short I wish she would have stuck with the horror aspect instead of trying to turn it into paranormal romance at the end. Had I known that was how it would be I would have passed on this book in the first place.<br /><br /><br />I probably won't recommend this book to my friends, but I would tell anyone interested in it to give it a try, because there are lots of people who enjoyed this book. It just wasn't for me. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17414124955394442770" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_217997930" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/217997930" />
    <a title="Catie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1886642-catie"><img alt="Catie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1385169623p2/1886642.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/217997930?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catie" href="/user/show/1886642-catie">Catie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1886642-catie?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1886642-catie?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1886642-catie?shelf=read-in-2011">read-in-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer217997930" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1113268956272986455">2 ½ stars<br/><br/>Ho hum. I hate it when this happens. You guys are all inside having a party with roasted chestnuts and hot cider and giant booming laughs and I am out here on a frigid winter’s night peering in through the frosty glass. (Oh yes. I <i>am</i> that dramatic.) But melodrama aside, I hate being the one to dislike something that everyone else loves. I’m sure we’ve all been here a time or two and it’s never fun. I'm not sure why I couldn't get into this one, but I am willing to admit that it may be b</span>
  <span id="freeText1113268956272986455" style="display:none">2 ½ stars<br /><br />Ho hum. I hate it when this happens. You guys are all inside having a party with roasted chestnuts and hot cider and giant booming laughs and I am out here on a frigid winter’s night peering in through the frosty glass. (Oh yes. I <i>am</i> that dramatic.) But melodrama aside, I hate being the one to dislike something that everyone else loves. I’m sure we’ve all been here a time or two and it’s never fun. I'm not sure why I couldn't get into this one, but I am willing to admit that it may be because I've just read a few amazing books in a row and everything else pales in comparison. But, I will try to explain my dissenting opinion about this one as best as I can. So here goes nothin.<br /><br />This whole book basically just made me wish I was watching an episode of Buffy the Vampire Slayer. Even Carmel helpfully brings it up at the end: Cas is Buffy, Thomas is Willow, and Carmel is Xander in a Cordelia suit. “Gideon” I just went ahead and referred to as Giles for the entire book. And obviously, Anna is Angel. However, where BtVS had conflict and depth as Ms. Summers tried in vain to balance her life as a slayer of all things evil with her life as a teenage girl, this book has none.<br /><br />Cas doesn’t have to worry about money, as his mom has a successful online business that easily travels from place to place. He doesn’t have to worry about his mother, who is largely absent and only seems to appear sporadically to heal Cas and provide herbal cookies. She also seems totally fine with letting him go off every night to battle ghosts. He doesn’t have to worry about his grades, as apparently the school he is enrolled in doesn’t require that he do any work or attend classes. He doesn’t have to worry about fitting in anywhere, because he has an endless supply of natural charm to pave his way. <br /><br />Cas says that he is a lone-wolf ghost hunter. The main struggle that he deals with is the struggle for real friendship and intimacy, something that he doesn’t have in his life. However, he seems to come by allies and aid quite easily (and conveniently) whenever he needs them in this story. While I did like the interactions between Cas, Thomas, and Carmel, none of them feel three dimensional to me. Thomas is the shy awkward supernatural kid and Carmel is the Queen Bee of the school. Their friendship seems shallow and flat. And the romance is completely dull and instantaneous. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cas literally goes from witnessing Anna rip a boy in half to swooning over her in a matter of days. And I CANNOT believe that he’s using the L-word by the end!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br /><br />The relationship feels a smidge healthier than most PNR’s (because they can essentially <i>both</i> kill each other at any time) but not by much. Anna is more complex than the stalkery vampire boyfriends, but she still has that inner core of violence and bloodlust that’s somehow caged by looooooove. Nothing makes my eyes roll more than that, I’m afraid. She can somehow hold it all in for Cas…but everyone else? Dead. <br /> <br />BUT, I did like Anna. She’s the main reason that I kept reading this and didn’t abandon it. I think that her history and motivations are very very interesting. I just wish that the romance part would go away.<br /><br />This book didn’t make me laugh and it never made me scared. It definitely doesn’t remind me of Hold Me Closer, Necromancer. Mainly, I just felt bored.<br /><br /><u>Perfect Musical Pairing</u><br /><br />Slow Runner – Spooky Ghost<br /><br />This song has a young feel that reminds me a lot of Cas. And it’s all about a spooky best friend...which is the relationship status that I wish could be applied to Anna and Cas.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1113268956272986455" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16628840-mario?shelf=own">own</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1074284417" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer6123683858764204581"><i>But hey, at least we’ll have this strange story to tell, love and death and blood and daddy-issues. And holy crap, I’m a psychiatrist’s wet dream.</i><br/><br/><br/>This book was so much better than I expected it to be. I expected a classic YA romance ghost story, but I got so much more. Surprisingly, romance played a small part in this novel, and that was refreshing to read. And none of the main characters annoyed me (especially the main character, Cas). And for a YA novel, that surprised me. <br/><br/>Also, this book was </span>
  <span id="freeText6123683858764204581" style="display:none"><i>But hey, at least we’ll have this strange story to tell, love and death and blood and daddy-issues. And holy crap, I’m a psychiatrist’s wet dream.</i><br /><br /><br />This book was so much better than I expected it to be. I expected a classic YA romance ghost story, but I got so much more. Surprisingly, romance played a small part in this novel, and that was refreshing to read. And none of the main characters annoyed me (especially the main character, Cas). And for a YA novel, that surprised me. <br /><br />Also, this book was <b>scary</b>. One scene, right at the beginning, even gave me nightmares. If that doesn't make you want to pick up and read this book I don't know what will.<br /><br />One more thing I want to mention is that for some reason (I don't even know why), sometimes I felt like I was reading <i>The Dresden Files</i> novel. They kind of had similar vibes. Also, main character reminded me a lot of Harry Dresden. <br /><br />And I'm so happy that this book have a sequel that I can immediately start. While I was reading, many times I've thought that this would make a great series, so I'm glad that it at least have one sequel. I just hope that it will be just as good as this one was, if not even better.</span>

<div id="review_206082392" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/206082392" />
    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2467655-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596119990p2/2467655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/206082392?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/2467655-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jo by: </span>
      MaWen
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer206082392" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12556623950094136413"><b> “You do know what we’re dealing with here, don’t you?” I ask. “She’s not just a ghost. She’s a hurricane. Overkill is fine by me.” </b><br/><br/><b>Initial Final Page Thoughts.</b><br/>I don’t know about something strange but there’s definitely somethingin this neighborhood.<br/><br/><b>High Points. </b><br/>Cas. Anna. Telepathic Tagalongs. Girls with too much daylight about them. Bloody deaths. Ghosts. Ghostbustin'. Cool mamas. Daddy issues. Moody kitties. Attic Ladders. Hitchhikers. Prom dresses. Drip, drip, drip. Ghost stories. Small town</span>
  <span id="freeText12556623950094136413" style="display:none"><b> “You do know what we’re dealing with here, don’t you?” I ask. “She’s not just a ghost. She’s a hurricane. Overkill is fine by me.” </b><br /><br /><b>Initial Final Page Thoughts.</b><br />I don’t know about something strange but there’s definitely somethingin this neighborhood.<br /><br /><b>High Points. </b><br />Cas. Anna. Telepathic Tagalongs. Girls with too much daylight about them. Bloody deaths. Ghosts. Ghostbustin'. Cool mamas. Daddy issues. Moody kitties. Attic Ladders. Hitchhikers. Prom dresses. Drip, drip, drip. Ghost stories. Small towns. Voodoo. Flashbacks. Basement lightshows. Things that go bump in the night. <br /><br /><b>Low Points</b>.<br />OK, if there are lots of ghosts running around America and killing people… why haven’t people cottoned on yet? What are the police doing? Why aren’t there as many exorcists as there are Starbucks? Why isn’t <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QN9p-XCCRwU&amp;feature=related%20" rel="nofollow noopener">this song</a> blasted out from public buildings to make people aware that there is a 98% chance that a ghost is going to eat them whenever they leave their house?<br />….just a thought.<br />Also, I’m pretty sure even Demi Moore would have rolled her eyes at some bits...but I'll get to that. <br /><b><br />Hero.</b><br />I’m just going throw this out there… I. loved. Cas.<br />I adore reading YA books that are told from a male perspective because there are so few, it’s always refreshing. <br />The girls really do like getting their voices heard, don’t they?<br />Anyway back to Cas.<br />It seemingly doesn’t take much for me to fall in love with a fictional boy, but referring to yourself as Rorschach will <i>always</i> work. You’re funny, you’re a badass, you’re fit (but my gosh, don’t you just know it), you’re cynical, you’re smart and you have this great, easy way of narrating. <br />Also, I genuinely believed that you could kill a ghost with a BAMF knife and not cry afterwards.<br />Which, in your career, is important. <br />Also, you look after your mum. Which is just lovely. <br />But your taste in women… I won’t go into it. <br /><br /><br />Oh, who am I kidding? Of <i>course</i>, I’ll go into it. <br /><b><br />Heroine.</b><br />In the beginning: YES YES A THOUSAND TIMES YES.<br />Seriously, amazing. Halloween costume= sorted. <br />At the end: The <i>true</i> Anna would pluck my eyes out if she could see how often they were rolling in my skull. Let’s go back please?<br /><b><br />Love Interest.</b><br />Ooooooooh myyyyyy loooooove, my darrrrrrlin’… I hunger for youuuuuuur touch<br />Yeah. I could have done without <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZoEwR9_Sy_M" rel="nofollow noopener">this</a> whole business.<br />I mean even if it was <i>physically</i> possible… would it even be <i>legal</i>?!<br />The mind boggles. BOGGLES, I SAY. <br />I wouldn’t say it ruined the book for me… but it definitely stopped me from jumping on a plane and hotfooting it to Canada to sit on Cas’ doorstep to await instructions on his next adventure.<br />I hope the sequel kind of just forgets about this… because I have no idea what I’m going to do with the khaki jumpsuit with the Ghostbusters patch that I sewed onto the front pocket. <br />Make your mind up whether I’m kidding or not. <br /><br /><br /><br /><b>Theme Tune.</b><br /><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4M7vpB-4zvM&amp;feature=related" rel="nofollow noopener">I'm Not Afraid by Howling Bells.</a><br /><br /><br /><b>Girl Angst Level</b><br />Difficult to come up with a number here because Cas is, at the moment anyway, cool as a cucumber. I can't imagine him turning into a serious, moody, broody boyfriend who believes in undying love (HA, geddit?)... but I've been proven wrong before.<br />So please please please let Cas maintain his awesomeness in the sequel and steer clear of the angst. <br />Because at the end of the day GhostGirl Angst is <i>still</i> Girl Angst. <br /><br /><b><br />Sadness Scale.</b><br />8/10. Oh Anna. That bit… you know, <i>that</i> bit. So sad.<br />Also, Ms Blake, one of the most fascinating and original way of using a flashback in a book! Wow. <br />Also, I need to stop getting emotionally attached to fictional critters. <br />I’m really intrigued about Cas’ backstory, especially concerning his dad. I think we’re going to have an interesting ride in the sequel. <br />And when I say interesting I mean me sobbing into a pillow. <br /><br /><b><br />Jo’s Scaredy Cat Rating.</b><br />7/10.<br />This was a genuinely creepy book, but I guess I was expecting more.<br /><br /><b><br />Recommended For.</b><br />People who don’t think twice picking up hitchhikers… even if they are dead. People who don’t mind sleeping with the light on. People who would always take Caspar’s side. People who hate it when magic gets so damn fruity. People who can’t wear white dresses without managing to spill something down them and staining them forever. Sigh. <br /><br />You can find this review and other exciting things on my blog <a href="http://weartheoldcoat.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12556623950094136413" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1691886079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9871318540888208977">This was pretty good. <br/><br/>It's perfect for people who want a light and easy paranormal read that happens to be a teen urban fantasy, rather than a teen urban fantasy that has paranormal elements.<br/><br/>For me, that focus is key. I like ghost stories, and while this one isn't particularly scary, it does manage to be fun, full of magic, a bit of mystery, and interesting characters. It's pretty popcorn and a pleasant way to spend a morning. :)<br/><br/>Nothing deep, just ghost hunting with high schoolers. :)</span>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1071520005" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7844203088224189950">This book was truly amazing. It was a one of a kind book with a unique plot. While reading this book, I couldn’t help thinking of Dean and Sam from Supernatural. Cas is a ghost killer who goes all over North America to kill harmful ghosts. When he seeks out Anna Korlov or “Anna Dressed In blood,” Cas encounters something different than he is used to. <br/><br/>The characters featured in this book are unique, well written, and are nothing typical. Blake was not afraid to break out of the norm having both t</span>
  <span id="freeText7844203088224189950" style="display:none">This book was truly amazing. It was a one of a kind book with a unique plot. While reading this book, I couldn’t help thinking of Dean and Sam from Supernatural. Cas is a ghost killer who goes all over North America to kill harmful ghosts. When he seeks out Anna Korlov or “Anna Dressed In blood,” Cas encounters something different than he is used to. <br /><br />The characters featured in this book are unique, well written, and are nothing typical. Blake was not afraid to break out of the norm having both tough and weak male characters, as well as female characters who are equally tough and weak. There are no minor characters. Everyone is equally important and none are more developed than others. <br /><br />Another really good feature of this book was that there was almost no focus on a love interest, and no weird drama. Most books now have some sort of drama between main characters that creates some sort of tension, however Anna Dressed In Blood was entirely focused on the plot and not on the useless side stories. <br /><br />Overall, I really loved the plot and concept of this book. A ghost, a tragic backstory, a haunted house and Canada as the main setting really sealed the deal on my love for this book. I definitely recommend it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7844203088224189950" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_201528907" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="HeatherJay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5969410-heatherjay"><img alt="HeatherJay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529554632p2/5969410.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="HeatherJay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="HeatherJay" href="/user/show/5969410-heatherjay">HeatherJay</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer201528907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4494827883901587603">When I was 13, my best friend, I'll call her Evil Kristin, thought it would be funny to scare the living shit out of me. Unfortunately, she decided to make this a regular occurence as scaring me was so very entertaining.I remember at a sleepover her mother had recently bought the hardcover of the book "The Exorcist". She put it right next to my pillow so that when I woke up it would be staring at me. For those who have never seen the book, here you go:<br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/the%20exorcist%20book%20cover/ferrerzg/TheExorcist--BookCover.jpg?o=0' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357518i/708799.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>The next morning I turned over and stare</span>
  <span id="freeText4494827883901587603" style="display:none">When I was 13, my best friend, I'll call her Evil Kristin, thought it would be funny to scare the living shit out of me. Unfortunately, she decided to make this a regular occurence as scaring me was so very entertaining.I remember at a sleepover her mother had recently bought the hardcover of the book "The Exorcist". She put it right next to my pillow so that when I woke up it would be staring at me. For those who have never seen the book, here you go:<br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/the%20exorcist%20book%20cover/ferrerzg/TheExorcist--BookCover.jpg?o=0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357518i/708799.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>The next morning I turned over and stared into the eyes of horror and screamed so loud her Siamese cat vaulted off the bed and face-planted into the closed bedroom door.<br><br>Good Times!<br><br>Evil Kristin continued on her "Pussification of Heather Tour" throughout our teens. Her most binding "prank" was forcing me to watch The Shining. I recall her telling me she had watched it with her brother and it had a "really sweet ending". Everytime I would get up to use the bathroom, she would screech "REDRUM, REDRUM!" and I would usually haul ass back to the bed either slamming my toe into the bedpost or kneeing the dresser at full speed.It was well into my thirties before I would go alone to fill the ice bucket at a hotel.<br>Anna Dressed in Blood regurgitated similar feelings in me but without the embarassing, teenage self-consciousness that always followed. <br>Our fearless leader, Cas Lowood kills the dead that cannot cross over. Cas and his mother move from place to place ridding the towns of whatever evil spirit is wreaking havoc on it's citizens.They move to Thunder Bay, Ontario where the ghost of Anna Korlov is rumored to have slaughtered countless trespassers who have dared to seek refuge in the dilapidated house that she resides in. What follows is a freaky, sweet, endearing and at times, scary as FUCK horror story. As Cas has spent his life moving around, he struggles with creating attachments to his highschool friends and to Anna as well, because Anna is different than the rest of the ghosts he has killed. In spite of my obvious squeamishness to anything scary, I had a blast with this book. The characters were likeable, the dialogue was witty and well-written and the plot moved along seamlessly. I'm glad there is a sequel in the works as I would hate to think I wouldn't be hearing from Cas again. </span>

<div id="review_1206276978" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1206276978" />
    <a title="Maggie ☘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40477684-maggie"><img alt="Maggie ☘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591529603p2/40477684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1206276978?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maggie ☘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maggie ☘" href="/user/show/40477684-maggie">Maggie ☘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40477684-maggie?shelf=great-reads-2017">great-reads-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40477684-maggie?shelf=paranormal-urban-fantasy">paranormal-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40477684-maggie?shelf=witches-magicians">witches-magicians</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1206276978" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7850050583307469593"><b>*3.8/5 hauuunting stars*</b> <br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Yes. Smashing. You’ll be just like those four chaps in the movie. You know the one, with the oversized marshmallow.”</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Anna Dressed in Blood</i> was such a <b>deliciously creepy</b> read which sends shivers down your back and makes you wary of walking dark hallways of your home at night. Yet, it wasn't the <i>'scared out of your mind'</i> type of story like those damned horror movies, it's still YA after all. <br/><i>Confession time</i>: I <b>HATE</b> horror movies. I think they are stupid and drastic and</span>
  <span id="freeText7850050583307469593" style="display:none"><b>*3.8/5 hauuunting stars*</b> <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Yes. Smashing. You’ll be just like those four chaps in the movie. You know the one, with the oversized marshmallow.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>Anna Dressed in Blood</i> was such a <b>deliciously creepy</b> read which sends shivers down your back and makes you wary of walking dark hallways of your home at night. Yet, it wasn't the <i>'scared out of your mind'</i> type of story like those damned horror movies, it's still YA after all. <br /><i>Confession time</i>: I <b>HATE</b> horror movies. I think they are stupid and drastic and I don't like to be scared out of my mind for days after. But I really enjoyed this book, it's more of a mix of paranormal with some horror aspects. It's very <b>atmospheric story</b>, <b>haunting</b> almost. <br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Don’t be afraid of the dark, Cas. But don’t let them tell you that everything that’s there in the dark is also there in the light. It isn’t.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />The simple way this book was told makes it so <b>easy to get through</b>, you won't even notice and half of the book is already behind you. The storyline is greatly plotted and flows effortlesly. There are also some intriguing plot twist. <b>Blake's storytelling simply pulls you in.</b> At first, you might think that there's nothing impressive about the writing style, yet there's this <b>quiet magic</b> about it that can't be descibed. It's just so easy to read and pretty clever. <b>Cas's voice actually sounds like a real teenage guy</b> without him acting like an asshole. <br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Over the course of my life I've been to lots of places. Shadowed places where things have gone wrong. Sinister places where things still are. I always hate the sunlit towns, full of newly built developments with double-car garages in shades of pale eggshell, surrounded by green lawns and dotted with laughing children. Those towns aren't any less haunted than the others. They're just better liars.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br /><b>The cast of characters was very likeable.</b> (Including one incredibly realistic cat who, of course, thinks he's the master of the world.) I know some people didn't like Cas, the main character, because he's supposedly full of himself and thinks himself above normal teenagers and high school issues. But I disagree. I think <b>he's realistic, flawed</b> and the way he lives made him into the person he is now. And I don't think that he thinks of himself above normal teens, he's separating himself from them, because his life as a ghost hunter is just different and he constantly moves on from one place to another. That makes him <b>independent, emotionally distanced, detached and brooding</b> at times (and yes, maybe a bit of a misanthrope at the beginning). <br />I don't know why, but <b>Cas, his imperfect voice and sarcastic humor resonated with me perfectly</b>.<br /><br /> <br /><i>
  <b>“But hey, at least we’ll have this strange story to tell, love and death and blood and daddy-issues. And holy crap, I’m a psychiatrist’s wet dream.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ <br /><br /> <br /><i>
  <b>“Smells like a Bob Marley concert in here.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />I was also quite <b>fascinated with Anna</b>. Her <b>tortured</b> character with dark past. Her self blame and hate. <b>Uncontrollable fits of murderous rage yet certain delicacy.</b> I feel like her character has even more potential than was shown to us and really hope that progression is made in the sequel. Truth be told, ghosts aren't really my idea of swoony love-interests, still <b>Cas and Anna's relationship was slow and moving</b> and made me hope for more. <br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I can feel that photo of Anna staring at me from sixty years ago, and I can’t help myself from wanting to protect her, wanting to save her from becoming what she already is.”</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ ✨ <br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I watch this girl, struggling to escape, not just from Elias’s grip, but from everything, from this stifling house, from this life like a weight around her shoulders, dragging her down and planting her in dirt.”</b>
</i><br /><br />The ending makes me desperate to dive headfirst into the finale. Highly recommended for <i>Supernatural</i> fans.<br /><br />P.S. We need more YA books from male POVs asap.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Anna, my strong, terrifying Anna.”</b>
</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7850050583307469593" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_150596893" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/150596893" />
    <a title="Giselle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle"><img alt="Giselle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1310159877p2/4800103.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/150596893?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giselle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giselle" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle">Giselle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781429982818" href="/book/show/11517203-anna-dressed-in-blood">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4800103-giselle?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer150596893" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10709770478654225224">Anna Dressed in Blood is YA meet <i>Amityville Horror</i>. It was creepy and ominous, but also funny. I didn't find it incredibly scary, just kind of spooky - well ok, a lot spooky. I did love it though, I absolutely did!<br/><br/>Firstly, it was refreshing to have a male protagonist. I wish there were more books as such. Theseus Cassio (Cas) is our main character in this novel and he's awesome! He has a great sense of humour and he's such a sweetheart. I adored his character. He's had a tough life being a ghost</span>
  <span id="freeText10709770478654225224" style="display:none">Anna Dressed in Blood is YA meet <i>Amityville Horror</i>. It was creepy and ominous, but also funny. I didn't find it incredibly scary, just kind of spooky - well ok, a lot spooky. I did love it though, I absolutely did!<br><br>Firstly, it was refreshing to have a male protagonist. I wish there were more books as such. Theseus Cassio (Cas) is our main character in this novel and he's awesome! He has a great sense of humour and he's such a sweetheart. I adored his character. He's had a tough life being a ghost hunter, but he makes light of his situations. He's also great at interacting with others. Unlike your stereotypical egocentric teenage boy. <br><br>Cas receives information regarding Anna, a ghost who's been murdering anyone who enters her house. All 27 people of them… so far. Subsequently, they pack up and move to her home town where Cas plans on stopping her. I loved the Anna story, it was typical but not cliché. I also loved how the author went beyond the usual YA and made it more graphic; more horrific. It really gives you the creeps!<br><br>I love my horror, this was 100% a book for me, and the author did a great job. Kendare knows how to tell a story, and tell it well. I didn't think it was over the top, but I could still see myself getting nightmares from this story. She gives us enough details to make us experience it - which considerably adds to the creep factor. There were a few minor traits that bothered me though. Mostly, it's the reaction of the characters that were often unconvincing: Anna, who is scary as heck, attacks and almost kills Carmel, and all she says is "My god, she's awful".. yeah.. a little...<br><br><i>"You forgot about the bad part. You know, the part where we have to get Anna inside the circle and throw chicken feet at her."</i><br><br>Another noteworthy aspect in this novel is the humour that is mixed in with the horror. Cas is funny and witty even in the worst situations. He knows his stuff, but he also sounds his age. This makes it all very easy to get into the story.<br><br>Ultimately, this is pure horror it's its finest form. If this wasn't enough to convince you to read it, just look at that cover and title. What's not to love?<br><br>--<br>For more of my reviews, visit my blog at <a href="http://www.xpressoreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Xpresso Reads</a> <a href="http://www.xpressoreads.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346185i/700655.png" width="380" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="10709770478654225224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11663424-anna-dressed-in-blood">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">cool people</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer195564701" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14334045902978047109">I started this with very high expectations. Everyone kept giving it high ratings, most of my friends were already reading it and talking about it between each other. I felt left alone! So I said f*ck it I’ll drop my current to-read list and start it. Good call that was.<br/><br/>Now how can I review <i>Anna Dressed in Blood</i> without acting like a total fangirl? Oh how about some pretty pictures that reflect my experience?<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380356182i/707925._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A-f*cking-mazing!! I was having the time of my life while reading this! <br/><br/>A love story betw</span>
  <span id="freeText14334045902978047109" style="display:none">I started this with very high expectations. Everyone kept giving it high ratings, most of my friends were already reading it and talking about it between each other. I felt left alone! So I said f*ck it I’ll drop my current to-read list and start it. Good call that was.<br><br>Now how can I review <i>Anna Dressed in Blood</i> without acting like a total fangirl? Oh how about some pretty pictures that reflect my experience?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380356182i/707925._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A-f*cking-mazing!! I was having the time of my life while reading this! <br><br>A love story between a boy and a ghost… That was a new one for me. Am I wrong for finding it romantic and not gross? Their <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[kiss <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> was the cutest thing ever! Cas is sooo badass, I developed a crush on him. I know I’m acting like a worked-up teenager over this book but I don’t care. I deserve this!!<br><br>I fell in love with the characters, fell in love with the town and fell in love with ghost stories again. It’s a wonderful feeling. And it got me searching for more books similar to this one (Hold Me Closer Necromancer is next on my list). Kendare Blake has such a brilliant mind. This won’t be the last book I read for her. And as for this series, I’m damn excited to read more. And btw 2012 is just cruel!<br><br>Oh, I think I found the perfect song for the book’s ending:<br><b><i>Wherever You Are</i> by Stream of Passion</b> <a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=4RmtQYWMIFM" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a>[link]<br><br><i>Favorite quote:</i><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m not a superhero,” I say. It’s an awful tag. It’s egotistical, and it doesn’t fit. I don’t parade around in spandex. I don’t do what I do and receive accolades and keys to cities. I work in the dark, killing what should have stayed dead.</i>
</blockquote><br>And relax, I haven’t forgotten about the surprised I promised. I did a little piece of fanart for my dear Anna. A three hour quickie, freehand, no references, Photoshop (as always). Hope you like!<br><br><a href="http://lh3.ggpht.com/-3fiH1m5igfM/TneY5GAj2SI/AAAAAAAAD0I/o5wgoAw38kI/s1600-h/Anna%25255B6%25255D.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380356182i/707926._SY540_.jpg" alt="image" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(click to enlarge)</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zy+vTn5Oqr69L7sBVfmR8P9QC+mEPetmm5gWO5snAVBi/bSeRDr3muTwN/jnRa55rjkUTCP9K4Miw9Rq6Na5nQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Xkuc/84GEA/W2iKTJIdFdJUouYWLxJ03yT/6dV5Ks97zmYcv9HJNK48FrmqWO3r9xEGmICwEXdJwZDgkLbsLEw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer16493774588815492353">So, I write books. The Anna Dressed in Blood duo is horror, The Goddess War trilogy is mythology, and Three Dark Crowns is fantasy, because the world don't move to the beat of just one drum. What might be right for you, may not be right for some. Love to read, too. Fiction, philosophy, good books, bad books, because you take the good you take the bad you take them both and there you have a stack o</span>
  <span id="freeText16493774588815492353" style="display:none">So, I write books. The Anna Dressed in Blood duo is horror, The Goddess War trilogy is mythology, and Three Dark Crowns is fantasy, because the world don't move to the beat of just one drum. What might be right for you, may not be right for some. Love to read, too. Fiction, philosophy, good books, bad books, because you take the good you take the bad you take them both and there you have a stack of books and stuff. I mean, you've got to be adventurous. There's more to life that what you're living, so take a chance and face the wind. <br /><br />There's more coming soon like ALL THESE BODIES and a new fantasy series, so don't waste another minute on your cryin. We're nowhere near the end. <br /><br />My likes include animals, food, and nostalgia. I mean, whatever happened to predictability? The milkman, the paperboy, the evening TV? Used to be everywhere you look, there's a heart, a hand to hold on to.<br /><br />Anyway, I love to hear from readers so drop me a line here or at my website and we'll talk about friends to know, and ways to grow, and how if you threw a party you would see that the biggest gift would be from me and the card attached would say, thank you for being a friend.<br /><br />We can also talk about all the sitcom theme songs in this bio. Sha la la la.</span>
